# @(#)OBDLYLAW.she	1.28 05:26:44 22/05/24  
# DESCRIPTION-- Daily backup schedule for lawson.
# DEPENDENCIES--
# CREATED -- 05/04/00 by J. Norris

SCHEDULE AMFINAN1#OBDLYLAW 
ON RUNCYCLE RULE1 "FREQ=DAILY"
AT 2000 
CARRYFORWARD
:
AMFINAN1#BSTOPLL
 FOLLOWS JDAPROD#JLOADLAW.@ 

ORAPRDP#BCTRLDLO
 FOLLOWS BSTOPLL

ORAPRDP#BSTPDLO
 FOLLOWS BCTRLDLO
 FOLLOWS BSTOPLL

#********* Create snapshots **********

AMFINAN1#BSNCRLPA
 FOLLOWS BSTOPLL

ORAPRDP#BSNCROPA
 FOLLOWS BSTPDLO

ORAPRDP#BSNCROPO
 FOLLOWS BSTPDLO

#********* Create Commvault Snapshots **********

AMFINAN1#COMMVAULT_START
 FOLLOWS BSNCRLPA
 FOLLOWS BSNCROPA
 FOLLOWS BSNCROPO
 FOLLOWS BSTOPLL
 FOLLOWS BSTPDLO

ORAPRDP#COMMVAULTO
 FOLLOWS BSNCROPA
 FOLLOWS BSNCROPO
 FOLLOWS BSTPDLO

AMFINAN1#COMMVAULTL
 FOLLOWS BSNCRLPA
 FOLLOWS BSTOPLL
 FOLLOWS BSTPDLO

AMFINAN1#COMMVAULT_END
 FOLLOWS COMMVAULTL
 FOLLOWS COMMVAULTO

#********* Start Lawson **********

ORAPRDP#BSTRDLO
 AT 2015 
 FOLLOWS BSNCROPA
 FOLLOWS BSNCROPO
 FOLLOWS BSTPDLO

AMFINAN1#BSTRTLL
 FOLLOWS BSNCRLPA
 FOLLOWS BSTRDLO
 FOLLOWS AMFINAN1#UTDELJOBHST.LAWLOGPRG 

#********* Delete snapshots **********

AMFINAN1#DELETE_SNAPS_PRI
 FOLLOWS BSTRTLL

AMFINAN1#DELETE_SNAPS_BKUP
 FOLLOWS BSTRTLL
END

 FOLLOWS DELETE_PRI_JDA

 FOLLOWS SHUTDOWN_JDAP

 FOLLOWS VERIFY_JDAP

 FOLLOWS SNAP_JDA

 FOLLOWS START_JDAP

 AT 0500 
END

# E_I_PIB_PHY_ALL Schedule Definitions 
#
# File:    E_I_PIB_PHY_ALL.she
# Version: 1.8
# Date:    13/06/04
# Time:    15:12:11
#    
# OUTBOUND Extract and create Inventory Transaction based on Physical Inventory batches (##Bill, ##Credit)
#          NOTE* - JTRFRASH  defined in JDASCD1D.job script
#                - JUPLSTG91 defined in JDASCD1D.job script
#                - JUPLD2S91 defined in JDASCD1D.job script
#                - JUPLTR91  defined in JDASCD1D.job script
# Dependencies: 
# Runs Sunday at 1930
#

SCHEDULE AMMERCH1#E_I_PIB_PHY_ALL 
ON RUNCYCLE EOM DESCRIPTION "End of Month" "FREQ=MONTHLY;INTERVAL=1;BYMONTHDAY=-1"
ON RUNCYCLE RULE1 "FREQ=WEEKLY;BYDAY=SU"
AT 1930 
CARRYFORWARD
:
AMMERCH1#JDAXTR_PIB_PHY_JDA

 FOLLOWS JDAXTR_PIB_PHY_JDA

AMMERCH1#JDATRN_PIB_PHY_INV
 FOLLOWS JDAEXP_PIB_PHY_JDA

AMMERCH1#JTRFRASH
NEEDS 1 AMMERCH1#J9POLOCK

# MAIN Schedule 
#- File MAIN.she
#- Version 1.24
#- Date 16/05/10
#- Time 15:28:36
#-
#
# INBOUND & OUTBOUND
# This is the "main" schedule that runs nightly batch processing for sales and interface programs 
# It starts every day at 1900 and runs until about 6 AM 
# This schedules is a reconfiguration of JDASCD1D to process sales after all inventory processing is done
#

SCHEDULE AMMERCH1#MAIN 
ON RUNCYCLE RULE1 "FREQ=DAILY;"
AT 1900 
CARRYFORWARD
FOLLOWS AMMERCH1#JANALYZD.@ 
FOLLOWS AMMERCH1#JSQLTEST.@ 
FOLLOWS AMMERCH1#U_JDA_PRD_CHK.@ 
FOLLOWS AMMERCH1#BACKUP_JDA.START_JDAP 
:
AMMERCH1#JPLVBLSA

 FOLLOWS JOLVBLSA
 FOLLOWS JPLVBLSA

 FOLLOWS JCLEANIW

#

# @(#)HEMSEOD.she	1.11 08:32:31 15/05/17
# DESCRIPTION-- Creates POS order data tables for distribution to the stores
#           1.  hemescon01 converts data fro an external format to HeMS format
#           2.  run_hemhscr01 compares store file and if they have changed
#               builds a new version for the store
#           3.  run_hemhsstg01 stages files for the stores
# DEPENDENCIES-- NONE
# CREATED-- 04/29/99, MV

AT 1600

 UNTIL 0115 
 EVERY 0045

 UNTIL 0115 
 EVERY 0045
 FOLLOWS HEMSEOD1

 UNTIL 0115 
 EVERY 0045
 FOLLOWS CMHANLYZ
 FOLLOWS HEMSEOD1

AMTSPOS1#HEMSEOD3
 UNTIL 0115 
 EVERY 0045
 FOLLOWS HEMSEOD2

AMTSPOS1#HEMSEOD4
 UNTIL 0125 
 EVERY 0045
 FOLLOWS HEMSEOD3

AMTSPOS1#HEMSLASTEOD1
 AT 0140 

AMTSPOS1#HEMSLASTEOD2
 FOLLOWS HEMSLASTEOD1

AMTSPOS1#HEMSLASTEOD3
 FOLLOWS HEMSLASTEOD2

AMTSPOS1#HEMSLASTEOD4
 FOLLOWS HEMSLASTEOD3

 FOLLOWS HEMSLASTEOD3

 FOLLOWS HEMSLASTEOD3

 FOLLOWS HEMSLASTEOD3

 FOLLOWS SHUTDOWN_JDAP

 AT 1915

END

#                         they drop into their SSH folder on JDA and this utility moves
#                         it into the BATO folder and visa-versa.
#
# DEPENDENCIES: None
#
# Runs Daily at 1400
#

#   $Log[10]:

# CREATED -- 06/18/98 by JL COMSTOCK

# ALTERED -- 05/03/99 by JL COMSTOCK, Changed the execution times

END

#@(#) $Id: Sfinal.conf,v 7.56 1995/02/24 04:13:53 alanh viola_thunder $
#  This is a sample schedule for doing pre and post production
#  processing.  It assumes the start time is 6:00 a.m.
#
#  It is defined as CARRYFORWARD because it is executed across
#  production days.  This ensures that job statistics will be
#  collected for the schedule.
#
#  All of the job statements that follow use auto-documentation
#  keywords so the jobs will be documented by composer when the
#  schedule is added or modified in the mastsked file.

SCHEDULE TWSPROD#FINAL 
ON RUNCYCLE RULE1 "FREQ=DAILY;"
AT 0559 
CARRYFORWARD
FOLLOWS TWSPROD#FINAL.@ PREVIOUS
:
TWSPROD#STARTAPPSERVER

TWSPROD#MAKEPLAN
 FOLLOWS STARTAPPSERVER

TWSPROD#SWITCHPLAN
 FOLLOWS MAKEPLAN

TWSPROD#CREATEPOSTREPORTS
 FOLLOWS SWITCHPLAN

#  MakePlan creates tomorrow's production control file (Symnew). 
#  Then it runs reporter to print  pre-production reports.
#  The reports should be reviewed.
#  SwitchPlan stops batchman and runs stageman to: 1) carry forward incomplete schedules,
#  2) log the old Symphony file, 3) create the new Symphony and Sinfonia
#  files.  It then starts batchman.
#  CreatePostReports runs reporter to print post-production reports.
#  UpdateStats runs logman to log job statistics, and then
#  report8 to print the Job Histogram.

TWSPROD#UPDATESTATS
 FOLLOWS SWITCHPLAN
END
